ng-tns-c865572621-18"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><structured-content-container _ngcontent-ng-c961163833="" data-test-id="message-content" _nghost-ng-c1313109264="" class="ng-tns-c961163833-17 ng-star-inserted"><div _ngcontent-ng-c1313109264="" class="container"><message-content _ngcontent-ng-c1313109264="" _nghost-ng-c4141413871="" id="extended-response-message-content" class="ng-star-inserted"><div _ngcontent-ng-c4141413871="" inline-copy-host="" class="markdown markdown-main-panel enable-luminous-fast-follows stronger enable-updated-hr-color" id="extended-response-markdown-content" aria-live="off" aria-busy="false" dir="ltr" style="--animation-duration: 400ms; --fade-animation-function: ease-out;"><h1 data-path-to-node="0">Hızlı Fourier Dönüşümü (FFT) ve Dijital Ses İşlemedeki Uygulamaları: Kapsamlı ve Analitik Bir İnceleme</h1><h2 data-path-to-node="1">1. Giriş</h2><p data-path-to-node="2" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-63"><span data-path-to-node="2,0">Sayısal sinyal işleme (Dijital Sinyal İşleme - DSP), fiziksel dünyadan elde edilen sürekli verilerin dijital ortamda analiz edilebilir, değiştirilebilir ve sıkıştırılabilir biçimlere dönüştürülmesini sağlayan modern mühendisliğin en kritik dallarından biridir. Bu disiplinin kalbinde yer alan en temel araç, zaman veya uzay alanındaki sinyalleri frekans alanına taşıyan Fourier dönüşümüdür. Doğadaki pek çok sinyal, özellikle de akustik dalgalar ve ses sinyalleri, zaman ekseninde oldukça karmaşık ve düzensiz görünmelerine rağmen frekans ekseninde incelendiklerinde çok daha belirgin, ayrıştırılabilir ve yorumlanabilir örüntüler sunarlar</span><span data-path-to-node="2,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="1"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="2,2">. Akustik gürültünün bastırılmasından konuşma tanıma sistemlerine kadar pek çok teknoloji, sinyallerin frekans bileşenlerine ayrıştırılması prensibine dayanır.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-63 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-74 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; visibility: hidden;"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="container ng-tns-c2242951624-74 hide" jslog="220997;BardVeMetadataKey:[null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,[2,null,1]]" style="--carousel-content-height: 0px;"><!----><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="carousel-container ng-tns-c2242951624-74"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" resizeobserver="" class="carousel-content ng-tns-c2242951624-74"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-74 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-74 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><!----><!----></div></div><!----></div><!----></sources-carousel><!----><!----><!----></sources-carousel-inline></p><p data-path-to-node="3">Ayrık Fourier Dönüşümü (Discrete Fourier Transform - DFT), dijital olarak örneklenmiş sinyallerin frekans spektrumunu hesaplamak için kullanılan temel matematiksel yöntemdir. Ancak, doğrudan DFT hesabı büyük veri setleri için asimptotik olarak pratik değildir ve hesaplama karmaşıklığı donanım sınırlarını hızla aşar. Tam bu noktada, Hızlı Fourier Dönüşümü (Fast Fourier Transform - FFT) devreye girmektedir. FFT, DFT'nin matematiksel olarak eşdeğerini çok daha az işlem gücüyle hesaplayan algoritmalar ailesidir.</p><p data-path-to-node="4" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-64"><span data-path-to-node="4,0">Tarihsel perspektiften bakıldığında, FFT'nin temellerinin 1805 yılında Carl Friedrich Gauss tarafından asteroit yörüngelerinin (Pallas ve Juno) enterpolasyonunu yapmak amacıyla atıldığı bilinmektedir</span><span data-path-to-node="4,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="2"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="4,2">. Ancak Gauss'un çalışmaları ölümünden sonra ve Neo-Latince yayımlandığı için uzun süre bilim dünyasının dikkatinden kaçmıştır. Modern dönüm noktası ise 1965 yılında James W. Cooley ve John W. Tukey'in yayımladığı "An algorithm for the machine calculation of complex Fourier series" başlıklı makale ile gerçekleşmiştir</span><span data-path-to-node="4,3"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="3"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="4,4">. Soğuk Savaş döneminde, Sovyetler Birliği'nin nükleer denemelerini sismik sensörler aracılığıyla tespit etme ihtiyacı, devasa zaman serilerinin gerçek zamanlı analizini zorunlu kılmış ve Tukey'in algoritmik öngörüleri bu dönemde şekillenmiştir</span><span data-path-to-node="4,5"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-66 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-77 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; Matematiksel Temeller</h2><p data-path-to-node="8" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-67"><span data-path-to-node="8,0">Ses sinyalleri, doğaları gereği hava basıncındaki değişimlerin oluşturduğu sürekli (analog) dalgalardır. Bu sinyallerin bilgisayar ortamında işlenebilmesi ve matematiksel modellere oturtulabilmesi için öncelikle ayrık (dijital) dizilere dönüştürülmeleri gerekmektedir. Bir sinyalin dijitalleştirilmesi süreci, zaman ekseninde örnekleme (sampling) ve genlik ekseninde kuantalama (quantization) olmak üzere iki ana aşamadan oluşur</span><span data-path-to-node="8,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="10"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="8,2">.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; Örnekleme Frekansı ve Nyquist-Shannon Teoremi</h3><p data-path-to-node="10" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-68"><span data-path-to-node="10,0">Zaman alanında sürekli olan bir <span class="math-inline" data-math="x(t)" data-index-in-node="32"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">t</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> sinyali, belirli ardışık zaman aralıklarıyla (<span class="math-inline" data-math="T_s" data-index-in-node="83"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">T</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>) ölçülerek <span class="math-inline" data-math="x[n] = x(nT_s)" data-index-in-node="98"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mclose">]</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">T</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> ayrık dizisine dönüştürülür. Burada örnekleme frekansı, saniyede alınan örnek sayısı olarak <span class="math-inline" data-math="f_s = 1/T_s" data-index-in-node="205"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1076em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1/</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">T</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> formülü ile tanımlanır. Sinyalin içerdiği bilginin eksiksiz olarak dijital ortama aktarılabilmesi ve daha sonra Whittaker-Shannon enterpolasyon formülü (sinc fonksiyonları) kullanılarak kayıpsız bir şekilde orijinal analog sinyale geri çatılabilmesi (reconstruction) için Claude Shannon'un 1949 tarihli çığır açıcı makalesinde de detaylandırdığı Nyquist-Shannon Örnekleme Teoremi'nin şartlarının sağlanması zorunludur</span><span data-path-to-node="10,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="10"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="10,2">.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-68 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-79 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; visibility: hidden;"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="container ng-tns-c2242951624-79 hide" jslog="220997;BardVeMetadataKey:[null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,[3,null,1]]" style="--carousel-content-height: 0px;"><!----><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="carousel-container ng-tns-c2242951624-79"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" resizeobserver="" class="carousel-content ng-tns-c2242951624-79"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-79 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-79 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-79 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><!----><!----></div></div><!----></div><!----></sources-carousel><!----><!----><!----></sources-carousel-inline></p><p data-path-to-node="11">Bu teorem, bir sinyalin içerdiği en yüksek frekans bileşeni <span class="math-inline" data-math="B" data-index-in-node="60"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">B</span></span></span></span></span> (bant genişliği) olmak üzere, kayıpsız bir örnekleme için örnekleme frekansının minimum limitini şu şekilde belirler:</p><div data-path-to-node="12"><div class="math-block" data-math="f_s \geq 2B"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1076em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">≥</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">B</span></span></span></span></span></div></div><p data-path-to-node="13" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-69"><span data-path-to-node="13,0">Eğer bu temel matematiksel sınır ihlal edilirse ve örnekleme hızı yeterince yüksek seçilmezse (<span class="math-inline" data-math="f_s &lt; 2B" data-index-in-node="95"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1076em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">&lt;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0502em;">B</span></span></span></span></span>), "örtüşme" (aliasing) adı verilen sinyal bozulumu meydana gelir. Örtüşme durumunda sinyalin yüksek frekanslı bileşenleri, dijital spektrumda düşük frekanslı bileşenler (gölge frekanslar) gibi görünerek sinyalin orijinal yapısını onarılamaz biçimde bozar</span><span data-path-to-node="13,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="1"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="13,2">. İnsan kulağının duyabildiği en yüksek akustik frekans sınırı genellikle 20 kHz civarında kabul edildiğinden, modern dijital ses sistemlerinde Nyquist oranının üzerinde kalmak ve donanımsal anti-aliasing filtrelerine bir geçiş bandı (transition band) bırakmak amacıyla <span class="math-inline" data-math="f_s = 44.1" data-index-in-node="270"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1076em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: class="mord">44.1</span></span></span></span></span> kHz (CD standardı) veya <span class="math-inline" data-math="48" data-index-in-node="305"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">48</span></span></span></span></span> kHz (DVD/Video standardı) standart olarak kullanılmaktadır</span><span data-path-to-node="13,3"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote data-path-to-node="14">2.2. Ayrık Fourier Dönüşümü (DFT) Denklemi</h3><p data-path-to-node="15" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-70"><span data-path-to-node="15,0">Dijital olarak modellenmiş ve sınırlandırılmış bir ses sinyalinin frekans içeriğini bulmak için Ayrık Fourier Dönüşümü (DFT) kullanılır. DFT, temel olarak <span class="math-inline" data-math="N" data-index-in-node="155"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span></span></span></span></span> uzunluğundaki bir <span class="math-inline" data-math="x[n]" data-index-in-node="175"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> zaman dizisini, yine <span class="math-inline" data-math="N" data-index-in-node="201"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span></span></span></span></span> uzunluğundaki bir <span class="math-inline" data-math="X[k]" data-index-in-node="221"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">X</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0315em;">k</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> frekans dizisine eşleyen doğrusal bir dönüşümdür. Matematiksel olarak DFT şu şekilde ifade edilir</span><span data-path-to-node="15,1"><span><response-element class="" data-math="X[k]" data-index-in-node="13"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">X</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0315em;">k</span><span karmaşık genliğini ifade eder. Her bir frekans kutusu (bin), <span class="math-inline" data-math="\Delta f = f_s / N" data-index-in-node="119"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1076em;">f</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1076em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span></span></span></span></span> frekans çözünürlüğüne karşılık gelir</span><span data-path-to-node="17,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="1"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="17,2">. Bu dönüşüm, N boyutlu bir vektörün, N boyutlu ortogonal (dik) bir tabana (basis) izdüşümünün alınması olarak da düşünülebilir. Bu taban fonksiyonları, farklı frekanslardaki kompleks sinüsoidal dalgalardır.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-71 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-82 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; visibility: hidden;"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="container ng-tns-c2242951624-82 hide" jslog="220997;BardVeMetadataKey:[null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,[1,null,1]]" style="--carousel-content-height: 0px;"><!----><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="carousel-container ng-tns-c2242951624-82"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" resizeobserver="" class="carousel-content ng-tns-c2242951624-82"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-82 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><!----><!----></div></div><!----></div><!----></sources-carousel><!----><!----><!----></sources-carousel-inline></p><h3 data-path-to-node="18">2.3. Bir başka deyişle Fourier dönüşümü, "Bu karmaşık ses sinyalinin içinde, <span class="math-inline" data-math="k" data-index-in-node="218"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span></span> frekansındaki bir sinüs dalgası ne kadar yer tutmaktadır?" sorusunun matematiksel yanıtıdır. Dönüşüm sonucunda elde edilen <span class="math-inline" data-math="X[k]" data-index-in-node="343"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">X</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0315em;">k</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> dizisinin mutlak değeri veya genliği (<span class="math-inline" data-math="|X[k]|" data-index-in-node="386"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">∠</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">X</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0315em;">k</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>) o frekans bileşeninin zaman içindeki başlangıç konumunu gösterir</span><span data-path-to-node="21,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="1"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="21,2">.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; FFT'nin Böl-ve-Yönet Özyineleme Bağıntısı</h3><p data-path-to-node="23" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-74"><span data-path-to-node="23,0">DFT'nin standart hesaplama biçimi (doğrudan toplam), her bir <span class="math-inline" data-math="k" data-index-in-node="61"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0315em;">k</span></span></span></span></span> değeri için <span class="math-inline" data-math="N" data-index-in-node="75"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span></span></span></span></span> adet karmaşık çarpma ve toplama işlemi gerektirir. Toplamda <span class="math-inline" data-math="N" data-index-in-node="137"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span></span></span></span></span> adet frekans bileşeni hesaplandığından, algoritmanın toplam zaman karmaşıklığı <span class="math-inline" data-math="O(N^2)" data-index-in-node="218"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1.0641em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> seviyesindedir</span><span data-path-to-node="23,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="5"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="23,2">. Sinyal uzunluğu <span class="math-inline" data-math="N" data-index-in-node="18"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span></span></span></span></span> arttıkça hesaplama maliyeti parabolik olarak büyür ve gerçek zamanlı analizleri imkânsız hale getirir.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-74 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-85 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; visibility: hidden;"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="container ng-tns-c2242951624-85 hide" jslog="220997;BardVeMetadataKey:[null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,[2,null,1]]" style="--carousel-content-height: 0px;"><!----><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="carousel-container ng-tns-c2242951624-85"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" resizeobserver="" class="carousel-content ng-tns-c2242951624-85"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-85 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-85 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><!----><!----></div></div><!----></div><!----></sources-carousel><!----><!----><!----></sources-carousel-inline></p><p data-path-to-node="24" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-75"><span data-path-to-node="24,0">FFT algoritması, bu tıkanıklığı "böl-ve-yönet" (divide-and-conquer) stratejisi ile aşar. FFT, <span class="math-inline" data-math="N" data-index-in-node="94"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span></span></span></span></span> uzunluğundaki büyük bir DFT hesaplamasını, her biri <span class="math-inline" data-math="N/2" data-index-in-node="148"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span><span class="mord">/2</span></span></span></span></span> uzunluğunda olan iki alt DFT işlemine özyinelemeli (recursive) olarak böler. Bu bölme işlemi, alt dizilerin boyutu 1 olana kadar (trivial case) devam eder. FFT'nin asimptotik çalışma süresini karakterize eden böl-ve-yönet özyineleme bağıntısı matematiksel olarak şu şekilde ifade edilir</span><span data-path-to-node="24,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="2"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="24,2">:</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-75 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-86 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">O</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span></div></div><p data-path-to-node="26" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-76"><span data-path-to-node="26,0">Burada <span class="math-inline" data-math="O(n)" data-index-in-node="7"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">O</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> terimi, alttan gelen sonuçların yön faktörleri (<span class="math-inline" data-math="W_N" data-index-in-node="60"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.1389em;">W</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.1389em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>) kullanılarak birleştirilmesi (kelebek işlemi - butterfly operation) için gereken doğrusal zamanı temsil eder. Algoritma analizi literatüründeki Master Teoremi'ne göre, bu özyineleme bağıntısının kesin çözümü <span class="math-inline" data-math="O(n \log n)" data-index-in-node="273"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0278em;">O</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mop">lo<span style="margin-right: 0.0139em;">g</span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mclose">)</span></span></span></span></span> karmaşıklığına denktir. Bu radikal düşüş, ses gibi yüksek örnekleme oranlarına sahip sinyallerin gerçek zamanlı (real-time) olarak işlenebilmesinin arkasındaki yegâne güçtür</span><span data-path-to-node="26,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="3"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="26,2">.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-76 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-87 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; Algoritma Varyantları</h2><p data-path-to-node="28">FFT tek bir katı algoritma formülü değil, temelde hesaplama yükünü optimize eden akıllı matris çarpanlarına ayırma işlemlerinden oluşan bir algoritmalar kümesidir. Veri kümesinin uzunluğuna ve donanım mimarisinin kısıtlamalarına göre çok farklı yaklaşımlar geliştirilmiştir.</p><h3 data-path-to-node="29">3.1. Cooley-Tukey Radix-2 Algoritması</h3><p data-path-to-node="30" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-77"><span data-path-to-node="30,0">Sinyal uzunluğunun ikinin tam kuvveti olduğu (<span class="math-inline" data-math="N = 2^m" data-index-in-node="46"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6644em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">2</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6644em;"><span class="" style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>) durumlarda uygulanan ve literatürde en çok kabul gören algoritmaya Radix-2 FFT adı verilir. Cooley ve Tukey'in çığır açan makalesi tam olarak bu özel duruma ve genel bileşik sayılara odaklanmıştır</span><span data-path-to-node="30,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="6"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="30,2">. Veriyi ikiye bölme işleminin nerede yapıldığına göre iki ana türeve ayrılır:</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-77 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-88 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; visibility: hidden;"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="container ng-tns-c2242951624-88 hide" jslog="220997;BardVeMetadataKey:[null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,[2,null,1]]" style="--carousel-content-height: 0px;"><!----><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="carousel-container ng-tns-c2242951624-88"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" resizeobserver="" class="carousel-content ng-tns-c2242951624-88"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-88 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-88 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><!----><!----></div></div><!----></div><!----></sources-carousel><!----><!----><!----></sources-carousel-inline></p><h4 data-path-to-node="31">3.1.1. Zaman Alanında Kırınım (Decimation-in-Time - DIT)</h4><p data-path-to-node="32" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-78"><span data-path-to-node="32,0">Zaman alanında kırınım (DIT) algoritmasında, girdi sinyali (<span class="math-inline" data-math="x[n]" data-index-in-node="60"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>) çift indisli (<span class="math-inline" data-math="x[2m]" data-index-in-node="80"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>) ve tek indisli (<span class="math-inline" data-math="x[2m+1]" data-index-in-node="103"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord">2</span><span class="mord mathnormal">m</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>) alt dizilere ayrıştırılır</span><span data-path-to-node="32,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="11"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="32,2">. Ayrıştırma işlemi, sinyal en küçük yapı taşına (2 elemanlı alt parçalara) inene kadar devam eder. Son aşamada bu elemanlar, yön faktörleri ile çarpılıp toplanarak (kelebek işlemi) spektral bileşenler halinde geri birleştirilir.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" Frekans Alanında Kırınım (Decimation-in-Frequency - DIF)</h4><p data-path-to-node="36" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-80"><span data-path-to-node="36,0">DIF yaklaşımında, girdi sinyali indekslerine göre tek ve çift olarak ayrılmak yerine, dizinin doğrudan ilk yarısı ve ikinci yarısı (<span class="math-inline" data-math="x[0 \dots N/2-1]" data-index-in-node="132"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord">0</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span><span class="mord">/2</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span> ve <span class="math-inline" data-math="x[N/2 \dots N-1]" data-index-in-node="152"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">x</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span><span class="mord">/2</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="minner">…</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">1</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>) bloklar halinde ikiye bölünür</span><span data-path-to-node="36,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="11"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="36,2">. Girdi dizisi bellekte normal sırasındadır ancak çıktı frekans değerleri (<span class="math-inline" data-math="X[k]" data-index-in-node="75"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0785em;">X</span><span class="mopen">[</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.0315em;">k</span><span class="mclose">]</span></span></span></span></span>) bit-ters sıralı (bit-reversed) olarak oluşur. Pratik donanım uygulamalarında ve modern DSP mikroişlemcilerinde DIT ve DIF birbirine eşdeğer asimptotik hızlarda çalışır.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-80 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-91 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; Asal Faktör (Prime-Factor) ve Karmaşık Tabanlı Algoritmalar</h3><p data-path-to-node="38" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-81"><span data-path-to-node="38,0">Her zaman örneklem sayısını ikinin kuvveti şeklinde ayarlamak mümkün olmayabilir (örneğin LTE iletişim sistemlerinde <span class="math-inline" data-math="N=1536" data-index-in-node="117"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">1536</span></span></span></span></span> gibi boyutlar yaygındır)</span><span data-path-to-node="38,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="5"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="38,2">. Eğer <span class="math-inline" data-math="N" data-index-in-node="7"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span></span></span></span></span> ikinin tam kuvveti değilse, ancak aralarında asal sayıların çarpımı olarak (<span class="math-inline" data-math="N = N_1 \cdot N_2" data-index-in-node="85"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.109em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">1</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.109em;">N</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3011em;"><span class="" style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.109em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight">2</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span class=""></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>) ifade edilebiliyorsa, I.J. Good tarafından geliştirilen Asal Faktör Algoritması (Good-Thomas algoritması / PFA) kullanılır</span><span data-path-to-node="38,3"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="2"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="38,4">.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-82 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-93 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; Uygulama: Dijital Ses İşleme</h2><p data-path-to-node="41">Hızlı Fourier Dönüşümü algoritmaları, sadece teorik matematiksel formülasyonlar olmanın çok ötesinde; stüdyo akustik analizleri, ses sentezi (synthesizer), sinyal filtreleme ve adli bilişim (audio forensics) gibi alanların ana motorudur. Ancak sonsuz ve sürekli değişen ses sinyallerini analiz ederken, klasik FFT'nin önemli bir kör noktası ortaya çıkar.</p><h3 data-path-to-node="42">4.1. Kısa Zamanlı Fourier Dönüşümü (STFT) ve Spektrogramlar</h3><p data-path-to-node="43" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-83"><span data-path-to-node="43,0">Klasik bir DFT veya FFT, sinyalin tüm zaman aralığı boyunca sahip olduğu frekansları kusursuz şekilde verir, ancak <i data-path-to-node="43,0" data-index-in-node="115">hangi frekansın hangi anda</i> gerçekleştiğine dair (lokal zaman bilgisi) hiçbir veri sunmaz. Oysa müzik, doğa sesleri veya insan konuşması gibi sinyaller son derece zaman-bağımlıdır (non-stationary); frekans bileşenleri milisaniyeler içinde değişir</span><span data-path-to-node="43,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="19"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="43,2">. Sinyal işlemede Heisenberg belirsizlik ilkesinin bir analogu olan bu durum, zaman ve frekans çözünürlüklerinin aynı anda sonsuz hassasiyetle bilinemeyeceğini gösterir</span><span data-path-to-node="43,3"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="19"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="43,4">.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-83 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-94 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; visibility: hidden;"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="container ng-tns-c2242951624-94 hide" jslog="220997;BardVeMetadataKey:[null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,[3,null,1]]" style="--carousel-content-height: 0px;"><!----><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="carousel-container ng-tns-c2242951624-94"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" resizeobserver="" class="carousel-content ng-tns-c2242951624-94"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-94 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-94 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-94 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><!----><!----></div></div><!----></div><!----></sources-carousel><!----><!----><!----></sources-carousel-inline></p><p data-path-to-node="44" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-84"><span data-path-to-node="44,0">Bu sorunu çözmek için Kısa Zamanlı Fourier Dönüşümü (STFT) geliştirilmiştir. Ses sinyali, dar pencerelere (örneğin 20-40 ms uzunluğunda bloklara) bölünür. Her blok kendi içinde durağan (stationary) kabul edilerek ayrı ayrı FFT işlemine tabi tutulur. Pencereler, spektral kayıpları önlemek için belirli bir örtüşme (overlap, genelde %50 veya %75) oranı ile ardışık şekilde kaydırılarak (sliding window) uygulanır</span><span data-path-to-node="44,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="19"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="44,2">. Geniş pencereler frekans çözünürlüğünü artırıp zaman çözünürlüğünü düşürürken (darbant spektrogram), dar pencereler tam tersi etki yaratır (genişbant spektrogram). Ortaya çıkan bu iki boyutlu matrisin karesel büyüklüğü alınıp renk haritasına dönüştürüldüğünde, zaman-frekans uzayının en önemli görsel aracı olan <i data-path-to-node="44,2" data-index-in-node="314">spektrogram</i> elde edilir.</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; <button _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" aria-label="Daha Fazla Bilgi" aria-controls="sources" class="mat-mdc-tooltip-trigger button image-fade-on hide-from-message-actions" aria-expanded="false" aria-describedby="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-84 cdk-describedby-message-ng-1-23" jslog="220646;track:generic_click,impression" cdk-describedby-host="ng-1"><mat-icon _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" role="img" class="mat-icon notranslate symbol google-symbols mat-ligature-font mat-icon-no-color" aria-hidden="true" data-mat-icon-type="font" data-mat-icon-name="expand_more" fonticon="expand_more"></mat-icon></button><!----></span><!----><sources-carousel _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" id="sources" _nghost-ng-c2242951624="" class="ng-tns-c2242951624-95 lm-enabled hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted" style="display: flex; visibility: hidden;"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="container ng-tns-c2242951624-95 hide" jslog="220997;BardVeMetadataKey:[null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,null,[1,null,1]]" style="--carousel-content-height: 0px;"><!----><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" class="carousel-container ng-tns-c2242951624-95"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" resizeobserver="" class="carousel-content ng-tns-c2242951624-95"><div _ngcontent-ng-c2242951624="" data-test-id="sources-carousel-source" class="sources-carousel-source ng-tns-c2242951624-95 hide ng-star-inserted"><!----></div><!----><!----></div></div><!----></div><!----></sources-carousel><!----><!----><!----></sources-carousel-inline></p><h3 data-path-to-node="45">4.2. Mel-Frekansı Kepstrum Katsayıları (MFCC)</h3><p data-path-to-node="46" id="p-im_d3c489cef528ba76-85"><span data-path-to-node="46,0">Yapay zeka, otomatik konuşma (ASR) ve konuşmacı tanıma sistemlerinde FFT'nin en hayati kullanımlarından biri, makine öğrenmesi modelleri için temel özellik vektörü olan MFCC (Mel-Frequency Cepstral Coefficients) metriklerinin çıkarılmasıdır. İnsan kulağının duyarlılığı frekansa göre lineer bir ölçekte ilerlemez; düşük frekanslardaki küçük değişimlere çok hassas iken, yüksek frekanslarda bu algı logaritmik olarak zayıflar. MFCC algoritması, FFT çıktılarını insan işitme algısına birebir uyarlamak için şu yapısal adımları izler</span><span data-path-to-node="46,1"><span><response-element class="" ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER"><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><source-footnote _nghost-ng-c3813734663="" class="ng-star-inserted"><sup _ngcontent-ng-c3813734663="" class="superscript" data-turn-source-index="21"><!----></sup></source-footnote><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----><!----></response-element></span></span><span data-path-to-node="46,2">:</span><sources-carousel-inline ng-version="0.0.0-PLACEHOLDER" _nghost-ng-c891437214=""><!----><span _ngcontent-ng-c891437214="" hide-from-message-actions="" class="button-container hide-from-message-actions ng-star-inserted"> &nbsp; Bunu dengelemek ve ses yolunun (vocal tract) etkilerini nötralize etmek için sinyal <span class="math-inline" data-math="y(n) = x(n) - \alpha x(n-1)" data-index-in-node="183"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em;
